### Social
## União de forças para mudanças relevantes
Através de parcerias com o Instituto Phi, Instituto Órizon e Instituto Ambikira, a SPX Capital apoia desde 2014 projetos nas áreas de saúde, educação, geração de trabalho e renda, e inclusão social. São priorizados projetos financeiramente sustentáveis e de alto impacto social.
### Creche São Charbel
###### Petrópolis
Atende crianças com uma proposta educacional dedicada à construção do pensamento crítico e autônomo, oferecendo às crianças uma nova perspectiva por meio de vivências lúdicas, reflexivas e significativas.
##### Apoio SPX:
Reforma.
### Disque Denúncia
###### Manutenção do programa. Anos dos apoios: 2017 e 2018.
É uma central de atendimento especializada em atender a população que vivencia ou presencia ações criminosas. Os relatos recebidos através das ligações anônimas são recebidos e repassados às autoridades competentes com rapidez e eficácia para agirem. As ações dos órgãos responsáveis são monitoradas e os resultados cobrados regularmente.
##### Apoio SPX:
Rio de Janeiro
### E aí como é que fica
###### Rocinha
Creche com atendimento em horário integral que cuida de 65 crianças de até quatro anos de idade, na Rocinha, com uma equipe de 11 funcionários.
##### Apoio SPX:
Reforma da sede, com pintura e recuperação da fachada.
### Fundação do Rim
###### Botafogo e Engenho de Dentro
Promove ações que melhoram a qualidade de vida de crianças e jovens renais crônicos do Rio de Janeiro.
##### Apoio SPX:
Fisioterapia motora para crianças portadoras de doença renal.
### Fundação Jesus de Nazaré
###### Duque de Caxias
A Fundação foi criada em 1999 no intuito de atender crianças da comunidade de Nova Campinas, Duque de Caxias/RJ. Hoje ela atende a mais de 200 crianças carentes.
##### Apoio SPX:
Reformas estruturais.
### Fundação Santa Bárbara
###### Vila de Cava – Nova Iguaçu
Entidade sem fins lucrativos que cuida de cerca de crianças e adolescentes em situação de risco social, filhos e/ou órfãos de portadores do vírus HIV.
##### Apoio SPX:
Reformas estruturais nos banheiros, telhado entre outras.
### Hemorio
###### Centro
Atua na promoção da saúde das pessoas com doenças hematológicas e na assistência hemoterápica.
##### Apoio SPX:
Modernização estrutural da rede de refrigeração.
### IBMEC
###### Centro
Instituição privada de ensino superior que há mais de quatro décadas forma profissionais de excelência, com visão internacional e protagonismo na veia.
##### Apoio SPX:
Compra de material didático para alunos bolsistas.
### Imadel
###### Guapimirim e Magé
Acolhe crianças, adolescentes, famílias e comunidade em situação de risco social com diversas oficinas, como por exemplo: teatro, artesanato, culinária, reciclagem, biblioteca.
##### Apoio SPX:
Construção das estufas, dos viveiros e canteiros de compostagem, sistema de utilização de água de chuva.

## WEBSITE terms of use
This website is operated by SPX Gestão de Recursos Ltda., SPX Equities Gestão de Recursos Ltda. and SPX International Asset Management Ltd. (collectively, “SPX” or the “SPX Entities”).  
  
By using this website, you are agreeing to these terms of use. SPX may change these terms at any time without further notice to you, and you are responsible for periodically reviewing these terms for updates. Your continued use of this website constitutes agreement by you to all such changes.  
  
Information about investments  
  
The content of this website is for informational purposes only and is not intended to provide specific investment advice for you, and should not be relied upon in that regard. No representation is given that the products or services discussed on or accessible through this website are suitable for you or any particular investor. You should not act or rely on any information provided herein without seeking the advice of a professional.  
  
This website is not directed to any person in any jurisdiction where (by reason of that person’s nationality, residence or otherwise) the availability of the information contained herein is prohibited. It is the responsibility of any persons accessing this website to inform themselves of and to observe fully the applicable laws and regulations of their respective jurisdictions.  
  
No information provided on this website constitutes a solicitation, offer or recommendation to buy or sell shares of any investment fund managed or sponsored by any of the SPX Entities, nor should it be construed as such in any jurisdiction where such a solicitation, offer or recommendation would be illegal or which would subject the SPX Entities to any registration requirement within such jurisdiction that they have not separately undertaken. None of the SPX Entities is registered with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (the “SEC”) or with the Commodity Futures Trading Commission (the “CFTC”). Shares of investment funds managed or sponsored by SPX have not been registered with the SEC or the CFTC, and investors in such funds will not have the protections afforded by registration with the SEC or the CFTC.  
  
Your use of this website  
  
You must not misuse this website by knowingly introducing viruses, trojans, worms, logic bombs or other material that is malicious or technologically harmful. You must not attempt to gain unauthorised access to this website, the server on which it is stored or any server, computer or database connected to this website. You must not attack this website via a denial-of-service attack or a distributed denial-of service attack. SPX will report any such breach to the relevant law enforcement authorities and will co-operate with those authorities by disclosing your identity to them.  
  
You must not use any data mining, robots or similar data gathering or extraction programs or methods, whether automated or manual, to access, acquire, copy or monitor any portion of this website or any of its contents.

### ABOUT SPX
## NAVIGATING VOLATILITY, DISCIPLINED RISK MANAGEMENT AND CAPITAL PRESERVATION ARE PART OF OUR DNA.
In 2010, SPX Capital was founded by a group of investment professionals with an established track record of generating alpha. The firm aims to generate attractive returns for investors over the long-term through the combination of high-quality human capital, robust investment processes and ethical values.
Through a meritocratic partnership model, SPX Capital seeks to attract and retain highly skilled professionals. The firm’s culture encourages teamwork and rewards those who seek excellence in group results.
Consistent returns and capital preservation are central to the SPX Capital’s ethos. The firm believes in gradual and sustainable growth, with the objective of building a lasting, resilient organization.
##  Timeline

#### Macro Strategies
### 2012
#### Equities Strategies

### 2022

‹›
## OUR PRINCIPLES
#### Expertise
A culture that promotes specialization and expertise across every area of the firm.
#### Partnership and Meritocracy
A meritocratic partnership with a collaborative culture, where outstanding professionals will be recognized based on results.
#### Discipline and Resilience
Discipline in the management of investments and resilience in the search for long-term performance.
#### Client focus
We manage client capital with the same care and diligence as we do our own.
#### Alignment of Interests
The partners have a large amount of their wealth in the firm’s funds and are required to reinvest a majority of the distributed profits.
#### Ethical behavior
We believe that a strong ethical framework is essential for building a lasting business.

```
                    [descricao] => Marcelo Castro joined SPX in January 2020 as partner and portfolio manager. His focus is global macro, with emphasis on sovereign credit, currencies, interest rates of emerging market economies. Prior to SPX, he was a partner and portfolio manager at Pharo Management from September 2005 to July 2016, where he helped develop a framework of risk taking heavily reliant on quantitative economic research and portfolio optimization tools. He has also worked at BNP Paribas from 1998 to 2004, Bankers Trust (1993-1997) and Banco Icatu (1989-1993). His focus at these institutions was Latin American fixed income and currency instruments trading, with a research-based, bottom-up approach.

Mr. Castro received his B.S Economics from PUC-Rio in 1990 and a one-year specialization degree in pure mathematics at USP-IME in 2005.  In July 2019 he graduated from LSE with a MSc in Economics.  Additionally, he taught the fundamentals of finance at Ibmec College, São Paulo (2002-2004) and published articles in the _Handbook of Emerging Fixed Income and Currency Markets,_ edited by Fabozzi & Franco in 1998, _Investing in Emerging Fixed Income Markets_, edited by Fabozzi and Pilarinu (2002) and _Risco e Regulacao_ edited by Giambiagi and Garcia (2010).
```

#### Rogério Xavier 
Board of Directors Chairman  
Head of Rates
Founded SPX in 2010 after working for Banco de Investimentos Garantia (1985-88) and Banco BBM (1989-2010), where he was Head of the proprietary trading desk (1997-2007) and Executive Director of the Asset Management (2008-10). Graduated in business administration from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ), he is a board member of the Pontifical Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro Endowment (PUC-RJ) and the Mobility and Social Development Institute (IMDS). 
#### Bruno Marangoni 
Board of Directors  
CEO
Joined SPX as a partner in 2014. Began his career in 2004 as a trainee at Banco Pactual and in 2007 joined the Currencies Desk. Later became portfolio manager for the Currencies and Fixed Income Desk at JGP Gestão de Recursos. Left JGP in 2014. Graduated in production engineering from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). 
#### Bruno Pandolfi 
Board of Directors  
Head of FX
Founded SPX in 2010. Joined Banco BBM in 1996, becoming a partner in 2003. Appointed Chief Financial Officer in 2009. Left Banco BBM in 2010. Earned an MBA with emphasis in finance from Instituto Brasileiro de Mercado de Capitais (IBMEC-RJ). Graduated in electronic engineering from the Federal University of Rio de Janeiro (UFRJ). 
#### Daniel Schneider 
Board of Directors  
Head of Investor Relations
Founded SPX in 2010. Began his career in 1994 in Alcan Brazil’s Financial Department. Joined Banco BBM in 1996 and became a partner in 2003. Appointed Director, Fixed Income Funds, Asset Management, in 2009. Left Banco BBM in 2010. Graduated in business management from Fundação Getúlio Vargas in São Paulo (FGV-SP). 
#### Leonardo Linhares 
Board of Directors  
Head of Equities
Joined SPX as a partner in 2012. Began his career in 1994 at Banco BBM, where he became a partner in 2003. Appointed Director, Equity Funds, Asset Management, in 2009. Left Banco BBM in 2012. Graduated in economics from the Federal University of Rio de Janeiro (UFRJ). 
#### Marcelo Castro 
Board of Directors  
Head of Multi-Asset
Marcelo Castro joined SPX in January 2020 as partner and portfolio manager. His focus is global macro, with emphasis on sovereign credit, currencies, interest rates of emerging market economies. Prior to SPX, he was a partner and portfolio manager at Pharo Management from September 2005 to July 2016, where he helped develop a framework of risk taking heavily reliant on quantitative economic research and portfolio optimization tools. He has also worked at BNP Paribas from 1998 to 2004, Bankers Trust (1993-1997) and Banco Icatu (1989-1993). His focus at these institutions was Latin American fixed income and currency instruments trading, with a research-based, bottom-up approach. Mr. Castro received his B.S Economics from PUC-Rio in 1990 and a one-year specialization degree in pure mathematics at USP-IME in 2005. In July 2019 he graduated from LSE with a MSc in Economics. Additionally, he taught the fundamentals of finance at Ibmec College, São Paulo (2002-2004) and published articles in the  _Handbook of Emerging Fixed Income and Currency Markets,_ edited by Fabozzi & Franco in 1998,  _Investing in Emerging Fixed Income Markets_ , edited by Fabozzi and Pilarinu (2002) and  _Risco e Regulacao_ edited by Giambiagi and Garcia (2010). 
* * *
## Partners
#### Albano Franco 
Director and Head of EM Credit
Joined SPX in 2019. Began his career at Banco Pactual where he stayed for 15 years, becoming partner in 2012. Worked in the equity research team covering retail and food sectors. Joined UBS Pactual’s proprietary credit desk before assuming in 2008 as head of BTG Pactual Asset Management’s credit area, being responsible for all credit strategies and its dedicated funds. Worked at American Express Financial Advisors in Atlanta, USA. Franco holds a degree in finance from Georgia State University. 
#### Alexandre Rodrigues 
Multi-Strategy PM
Joined SPX in 2024, in the São Paulo’s office as a Partner at Multi-Strategy area. Alexandre has previous experience at Itaú, Canvas Capital, Banco Pan, BTG Pactual and Banco Brascan. He holds a degree in Electronic Engineering at Universidade Federal do Rio de Janeiro (UFRJ) and earned a master's degree in Economics at Instituto de Ensino e Pesquisa (INSPER). 
#### Beny Parnes 
Chief Economist North American & Asia
Joined SPX as a partner in 2013. Began his career at Banco BBM in 1991. Board member Head of the Central Bank of Brazil’s International Affairs Department between 2002 and 2003. Returned to Banco BBM in 2004 as an executive director and left again in 2013. Completed the credits for the doctoral program at the University of Pennsylvania (without concluding his thesis). Graduated in economics from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). Senior lecturer at this university’s Department of Economics. 
#### Bernardo Queiroz 
Director of Operations and Products, COO
Joined SPX as a partner in 2010. Began his career at Banco BBM’s back office in 2003. Left Banco BBM in 2010. Earned an MBA with emphasis in finance and capital markets from Fundação Getúlio Vargas (FGV-RJ). Graduated in business administration from Instituto Brasileiro de Mercado de Capitais (IBMEC-RJ). 
#### Bernardo Remy 
Investor Relations
Joined SPX as a partner in 2021. Before SPX, he worked at Pátria Investimentos, Bratus Capital, Partners Group and Aracruz Celulose. Remy earned an MBA from London Business School and a Bachelor’s Degree in Business Administration from Ibmec – RJ. 
#### Bruna Silveira 
Head of Equities Research
Joined SPX in 2012, becoming a partner in 2014. Began her career at Banco BBM in 2010, working in the Equities sector. In 2011, worked as Market Analyst. Graduated in Economics from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). 
#### Bruno Mafra 
Head of Quant
Joined SPX as a partner in 2010. Began his career at Banco BBM in 2004. Appointed portfolio manager of commodities desk in 2009. Left Banco BBM in 2010. Earned a master’s in finance from Instituto Nacional de Matemática Pura e Aplicada (IMPA). Graduated in electrical engineering from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ) and École Centrale de Paris. 
#### Diego Andrés 
Head of Quant Research
Joined SPX in 2019 as a quantitative analyst. He was a co-founder of Trapezus Asset Management in 2010 and partner at Bozano Investimentos / Crescera Investimentos. Diego holds a degree in Electronic Engineering from Instituto Militar de Engenharia (IME). He has a master degree in Mathematical Methods Applied to Finance at Instituto de Matemática Pura e Aplicada (IMPA). 
#### Edson Peli 
Director of Private Equity
Joined SPX in 2021 as a partner in Private Equity. Edson was a Managing Director at The Carlyle Group focused on private equity investments in South America, primarily in Brazil, for over 13 years. Since 2008 at Carlyle, he has directly participated in more than R$ 5 billion in equity investments from Carlyle’s funds in the healthcare, education and consumer & retail sectors. Prior to Carlyle, Edson worked in investment banking at Credit Suisse in Brazil from 2004 to 2008, where he participated in several M&A and IPO transactions across various sectors. Prior to that, Edson worked in credit risk analysis at Citi from 2002 to 2004. Edson graduated in Business Administration at Fundação Getúlio Vargas (FGV) and holds a Certificate of Specialization in Corporate Finance & Capital Markets at The University of Texas at Austin.
#### Eduardo Zilberman 
Senior Economist LatAm and Asia
Joined SPX in 2024 in the Rio de Janeiro’s office as a Partner and Latam Senior Economist at Macro area. Eduardo has previous experience at Gávea Investimentos, PUC and Central Bank of Chile. He holds a degree and a master’s in Economics from Pontifícia Universidade Católica (PUC) and a doctorate in Economics from New York University (NYU). 
#### Federico Favero 
Head of IT and Technology
Joined SPX in 2019 an analyst at Credit Risk Area. He has previous experience at Brain Brane (Italy), Snell Habitat SPA (Italy), Evolutiq GMBH (Swiss), Banco BBM (Brazil). Federico graduated in Pure and Applied Mathematics at Universitá Degli Studi di Padova (Italy), he is also post-graduated in Advanced Risk and Portfolio Management (ARPM Bootcamp) from NY University (USA), and holds a Master’s Advanced Finance from IE Business School (Spain). 
#### Fernando Borges 
Director and Head of Private Equity
Joined SPX in 2021 as partner and head of Private Equity. Fernando was Head of Carlyle South America Buyout. He has 25 years of private equity experience in Brazil, having participated in over 20 transactions and served on many of the boards of Carlyle’s local portfolio companies. He is also a former Chairman of ABVCAP, the Brazilian Private Equity & Venture Capital Association. Prior to joining Carlyle, Fernando was Managing Director of AIG Capital Partners and CEO of AIG Capital Investments do Brasil, responsible for managing AIG’s private equity assets in Brazil. From 1994 to 1999, he was a Principal of Bozano, Simonsen’s private equity division. Fernando graduated in International Relations at Universidade de Brasília (UnB). 
#### Gabriel Hartung 
Head of Rates Brazil
Joined SPX as a partner in 2013. Began his career at Instituto Brasileiro de Economia (IBRE) in 2006. Joined Banco BBM’s Macroeconomic Research team in 2008, leaving in 2013. Earned a PhD and master’s from Fundação Getúlio Vargas (EPGE/FGV). Graduated in economics from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). 
#### Guilherme Mazie 
CFO
Joined SPX in 2012, becoming a partner in 2013. Began his career at Banco BBM in 2009, researching quantitative models. Appointed equities fund portfolio manager in 2011. Left Banco BBM in 2012. Graduated in production engineering from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). 
#### Gustavo Rabello 
FX Senior PM
Joined SPX in 2015 on the Macroeconomic Research Team and later became a currency analyst. In 2017 became a Currency Trader. Rabello holds a master’s degree in Economics from Getúlio Vargas Foundation (FGV) and graduated in Economics from the Federal University of Rio de Janeiro (UFRJ). 
#### James Brilliant 
Legal & Compliance Senior Manager
Joined SPX in 2017. From 2012 to 2017, he held senior compliance positions at Nomura International, Capula Investment Management and Winton Capital, and from 2004 to 2012 he practised as a regulatory lawyer, first at the English Bar and then with law firms Shearman & Sterling and Kirkland & Ellis. Graduated from Oxford University with a degree in Classics. 
#### James Eckrich 
Investor Relations
Joined SPX in 2017 and became a partner in 2022. Began his career at Morgan Stanley in NY and in 2009 was transferred to London. In 2012 he joined the investor relations team at JGP Global, working out of their headquarters in Rio de Janeiro. Mr. Eckrich graduated with a degree in Business Administration and Finance from University of Richmond, USA. 
#### João Faria 
Senior Economist Europe
Joined SPX in 2015. Started his career as Projectl Manager at the Ministry of Development, Industry and Foreign Trade. He holds a degree in International Relations from UnB and a Masters in Economics from EPGE / FGV. 
#### João Victor Torres 
Equities Longs Senior PM
Joined SPX in 2016. He started his career with an internship in the stock exchange area. João holds a degree in Economics from PUC Rio. 
#### Katherine Albuquerque 
Director of Legal and Compliance, GC & CCO
Joined SPX as a partner in 2014. Began her career at Banco BBM in 1997, working in Corporate / Fiscal areas. In 2009 joined EBX working initially the Legal Department, as well as in the banking, corporate and tax areas. Earned an MBA with emphasis in finance and specialization in tax law from Getúlio Vargas Foundation (FGV-RJ). Graduated in law school from Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). 
#### Kym Ardison 
Currency Senior PM
Joined SPX in 2017. Began her career as an intern at Ativa Corretora. Worked at Dimensional Fund Advisors (Texas) in the summer internship program for PhDs. Ardison has a degree in Economics from FUCAPE Business School, a master’s and a PhD in Economics from Brazilian School of Economics and Finance (EPGE – FGV). 
#### Leonardo Cabral 
Director of Risk and Pricing, CRO
Joined SPX as a partner in 2014. Began your career at Banco Cindam em 1995, working in the interest rates and currencies trading desk. Worked in London at Deutsche Bank (2004-2009) in the FX derivatives trading desk and at Barclays as director of the FX Correlation trading desk. In 2011, returned to Brazil as a partner at JGP Gestão de Recursos, working as Senior Curriencies Portfolio Manager. Earned an MBA from Wharton – University of Pennsylvania – with emphasis in finance and accounting in 2005. Graduated in Mechanical Engeneering from the Federal University of Rio de Janeiro (UFRJ). 
#### Leonardo Lima 
Equities Longs Research Senior Manager
Joined SPX in 2018. Started his career as an intern at Consórcio Construtor Rio Barra. In 2017, he interned in the Wealth Management area and became an Equity Analyst at Rapier Investimentos. Assumed the position of Equity Analyst at Meta Management. Lima holds a degree in Civil Engineering from PUC Rio. 
#### Luis Cristofaro 
DM Rates Senior PM
Began his career at SPX in 2014 with the investor relations team, worked in the macro and commodities research teams before joining as a trader for the rates desk. Cristofaro graduated in production engineering from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). 
#### Luiz Caloba 
Head of Treasury & Execution
Joined SPX in 2022 as a Manager at the Liquid Funds Treasury division. Caloba has previous experience at Raizen, Banco BOCOM BBM, Goldman Sachs do Brasil, Banco BBM and at JSI Investment. He graduated in Naval Engineering at Universidade Federal do Rio de Janeiro (UFRJ) and earned a master's degree in Business Administration at COPPEAD/UFRJ. 
#### Marcella Libardoni 
Head of DM Rates
Joined SPX in 2011 as a macroeconomic analyst and later became an international interest portfolio manager. In 2017 she became a partner. Libardoni holds a degree in Economics from Fundação Getúlio Vargas (EPGE / FGV).
#### Marcelo Carletti 
Director of Real Estate
Joined SPX in 2021 as partner at JV SPX CCP in Real Estate Area. He has previous experience at Autonomy Investimentos, BR Properties, McDonald’s and at CB Richard Ellis. He graduated in Civil Engineering at Universidade Mackenzie, he has MBA in Real Estate from Escola Politécnica da Universidade de São Paulo (POLI-USP). 
#### Marilia Lorena 
Legal & Compliance Senior Manager
Joined SPX in 2018. Began her career at BNY Mellon in 2007, working in the Legal Department. From 2010 to 2012 worked as a foreigner lawyer in the Legal & Compliance Department at Newedge USA, LLC (NYC). In 2012 joined Cepeda Advogados as a senior lawyer. In 2013 worked as a Compliance and Internal Controls manager at JGP Gestão de Recursos. Earned a master’s degree in Business Law with emphasis in Banking and Tax Law from Getúlio Vargas Foundation (FGV). Holds a LLM in Financial Services Law – Asset Management from NY Law School (NY). Lorena graduated in Law from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC – RJ). 
#### Murilo Oliveira 
Head of Equities Brazil
Joined SPX as a partner in 2013. Began his career at Banco Itaú’s Department of Products for Individual Investors in 2006. Joined Banco BBM in 2008, working in Private Equity and M&A. Joined Banco BBM’s Equity Research team in 2009, leaving the bank in 2013. Graduated in electronic engineering from Instituto Tecnológico de Aeronáutica (ITA). 
#### Paula Ronchi 
Director of HR, Administration and Marketing, CHRO
Joined SPX in 2011. Began her career at IBM in 2010, working in the Global Financing sector. Ronchi graduated in Business Administration from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC – RJ). 
#### Pedro Daltro 
Director and Head of Real Estate
Joined SPX as a partner in 2021. Previously, he was a founding partner of BR Properties where he acted as CFO and member of Investor Relations from 2007 to 2015. In other past roles, he served as a Director in the Corporate Banking Area at Citigroup, where he was responsible for Public and Infrastructure sectors, as well as Financial Manager at Gafisa. Pedro Daltro earned his MBA from Vanderbilt University (USA). 
#### Rafael Godoy 
Head of Back Office and Middle
Joined SPX in 2018. He started his career as an intern at Banco BVA. In 2005 he became an Analyst at JGP Asset Management. He assumed the position of Senior Analyst at Banco UBS Pactual in 2007. At Triscorp Asset Management he was the Head of Operations in 2009. In 2011 he became a partner at Banco Brasil Plural. Godoy holds a degree in Economics from IBMEC Rio and a Master’s in Finance and Economics from IBMEC Rio and a Master’s in Finance and Econometrics from Queen Mary University of London (UK). 
#### Rafael Magri 
Chief Economist US
Joined SPX in 2015. Began his career at Opportuniyt Asset in 2010 as a macroeconomist. Graduated in Economics from UnB and earned masters in economics from PUC-RJ. 
#### Raphael Kruczan 
Rates PM
Joined SPX in 2017. Began his career at GE Oil & Gas. Kruczan graduated in Mechanical Engineering at UFRJ. 
#### Raphael Magrath 
Multi-Strategy PM
Joined SPX in 2015. Started his career as an intern at XP Investimentos in the Capital Markets area and at Visagio in the management engineering consultancy area. Magrath has a degree in Production Engineering from UFRJ. 
#### Rodrigo Godinho 
Head of Investor Relations
Joined SPX in 2010 and became a partner in 2011. Began his career at Banco BBM in 2001. Appointed Interest Rate Trader, Corporate Treasury, in 2005. Left Banco BBM in 2010. Earned an MBA with emphasis in finance and capital markets from Fundação Getúlio Vargas in Rio de Janeiro (FGV-RJ). Graduated in economics from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). 
#### Thiago Matera 
Equities Longs Research Senior Manager
Joined SPX in 2018. He started his career as an intern at Consultoria EloGroup and Banco BBM. In 2016 he became a Credit Analyst at Banco BBM. Matera holds a degree in Production Engineering from UFRJ. 
#### Tiago Fernandes 
Head of FX
Joined SPX in 2011 and became a partner in 2013. Began his career at Banco BBM in 2010, working in Market Risk. Left in 2011. Graduated in production engineering from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ) and management engineering from the Polytechnic University of Milan. 
#### Vinicius Hessel 
Quant Desk Senior PM
Joined SPX in 2020 as an analyst at Quantitative Research Area. He has previous experience at Trapezus Asset Management, Crescera Investimentos and at Loft. He graduated in Computer Engineering at Instituto Militar de Engenharia (IME) and has a master degree in Mathematical Methods Applied to Finance at Instituto de Matemática Pura e Aplicada (IMPA). 
#### William Bethlem 
Head of Business Development Asia
Joined SPX in 2022 as an head of Business Development. He has previous experience at Gow Capital, at Itaú Unibanco and Goldman Sachs. William graduated in Economic Science at Pontifícia Universidade Católica (PUC) and has a MBA at Harvard Business School.

## THE FIRM
Founded in 2010, SPX Capital is a global alternative asset manager offering investment strategies in macro, equity, credit, real estate and private equity. The firm aims to generate attractive returns for investors over the long-term through the combination of: 
#### high quality human capital, robust investment processes and ethical values.

## Termos e Condições do Website
Abaixo seguem algumas informações importantes sobre o material contido no website:  
  
As informações contidas neste website são de caráter meramente informativo e não constituem qualquer tipo de aconselhamento de investimentos, não devendo ser utilizadas para esta finalidade. Seu único propósito é dar transparência à gestão executada pela SPX Gestão de Recursos Ltda. (“SPX Capital”), SPX Private Equity Gestão de Recursos Ltda. (“SPX Private Equity”), SPX SYN Gestão de Recursos Ltda. (“SPX SYN”), SPX Soluções de Investimentos Ltda. ("SPX Soluções de Investimentos") e empresas do grupo SPX (“Grupo SPX”).  
  
Nenhuma informação contida neste website constitui uma solicitação, oferta ou recomendação para compra ou venda de quotas de fundos de investimento, ou de quaisquer outros valores mobiliários. O Grupo SPX não comercializa nem distribui quotas de fundos de investimento ou qualquer outro ativo financeiro. Recomendamos uma consulta a assessores de investimento e profissionais especializados para uma análise específica, personalizada antes de sua decisão sobre investimentos.  
  
Aos investidores, é recomendada a leitura cuidadosa de prospectos e regulamentos ao aplicar seus recursos.  
  
Este website não é direcionado para quem se encontrar proibido por lei a acessar as informações nele contidas, as quais não devem ser usadas de qualquer forma contrária a qualquer lei de qualquer jurisdição.  
  
Fundos de Investimento não contam com a garantia do administrador do fundo, do gestor da carteira, de qualquer mecanismo de seguro ou, ainda, do Fundo Garantidor de Créditos – FGC.  
  
Nos fundos geridos pelo Grupo SPX, a data de conversão de cotas pode ser diversa da data de aplicação e de resgate, e a data de pagamento do resgate pode ser diversa da data do pedido de resgate.  
  
A rentabilidade divulgada em determinados trechos do website já é líquida das taxas de administração, de performance e dos outros custos pertinentes ao fundo, mas não é líquida de impostos. Para avaliação da performance do fundo de investimento, é recomendável uma análise de, no mínimo, 12 (doze) meses. A rentabilidade obtida no passado não representa garantia de rentabilidade futura.  
  
Os fundos geridos pelo Grupo SPX podem utilizar estratégias com derivativos como parte integrante de sua política de investimento. Tais estratégias, da forma como são adotadas, podem resultar em significativas perdas patrimoniais para seus cotistas, podendo, inclusive, acarretar tanto perdas superiores ao capital aplicado, quanto uma consequente obrigação do cotista de aportar recursos adicionais para cobrir o prejuízo do fundo.  
  
Eventuais fundos geridos pelo Grupo SPX estão autorizados a realizar aplicações em ativos financeiros no exterior. Os fundos podem ainda estar expostos a uma significativa concentração em ativos de poucos emissores, com riscos daí decorrentes. Não há garantia de que os fundos multimercados terão o tratamento tributário para fundos de longo prazo.  
  
O Grupo SPX, seus administradores, sócios e funcionários não se responsabilizam pela publicação acidental de informações incorretas, e isentam-se de responsabilidade sobre quaisquer danos resultantes direta ou indiretamente da utilização das informações contidas neste website.  
  
O conteúdo deste website não pode ser copiado, reproduzido, publicado, retransmitido ou distribuído, no todo ou em parte, por qualquer meio e modo, sem a prévia e expressa autorização, por escrito, do Grupo SPX.

### fundos / 
# SPX Crédito Privado Prev
Descrição e características Arquivos
## Descrição e características
#### Objetivo
Fundo renda fixa com objetivo de proporcionar aos seus cotistas ganhos de capital no longo prazo.
#### Política de Investimento
O fundo segue a estratégia do SPX Seahawk, respeitando as restrições da regulação previdenciária.
Fundo de crédito privado de estratégia _long only_ e que possui alocação em ativos  _high grade_ (baixo risco de crédito). A carteira é composta por títulos de dívidas financeiras e corporativas de companhias de capital aberto, como debêntures, FIDCs, notas promissórias, letras financeiras, CDBs, entre outros instrumentos. O fundo tem como objetivo oferecer acesso às melhores oportunidades do mercado de crédito, se alavancando na gestão ativa e na sinergia com áreas de pesquisa macro e de ações da SPX.
#### Público Alvo
PGBL ou VGBL
#### Informações Gerais
Data de Início  17/06/2025   
Classificação Anbima  Previdência – Renda Fixa Duração Livre – Crédito Livre   
Aplicação Inicial Mínima  Não Há   
Movimentação mínima  Não Há   
Saldo Mínimo  Não Há   
Horário de Movimentação  15:30   
Cota de Aplicação  Cota do dia útil da disponibilidade dos recursos (D+0)   
Cota de Resgate  Cota de D+8 dias uteis após a solicitação de resgate   
Pagamento do Resgate  1º dia útil subsequente a conversão de cotas   
Taxa de Antecipação de Resgate  Não Há   
Taxa de Administração  0,7% a.a.¹   
Taxa de Performance  20% sobre o CDI (cobrada anualmente)²   
Gestores  SPX Gestão de Recursos Ltda.   
Administrador Intrag Distribuidora de Títulos e Valores Mobiliários Ltda   
Tributação  PGBL ou VGBL   
  1. Taxa de administração total de 0,70% a.a., sendo 0,28% a.a. incidente sobre os investimentos no FIQ, acrescido de 0,42% a.a. incidente sobre os investimentos Master
  2. O benchmark de performance efetivo é acrescido da Taxa de Administração do FIQ para permitir uma cobrança mais precisa.

The funds managed by SPX use derivatives strategies as an integral part of their investment policies. Such strategies, as adopted by the funds, may result in significant losses potentially exceeding the capital invested, obliging investors to deposit additional funds to cover such losses.

### ABOUT SPX
## NAVIGATING VOLATILITY, DISCIPLINED RISK MANAGEMENT AND CAPITAL PRESERVATION ARE PART OF OUR DNA.
In 2010, SPX Capital was founded by a group of investment professionals with an established track record of generating alpha. The firm aims to generate attractive returns for investors over the long-term through the combination of high-quality human capital, robust investment processes and ethical values.
Through a meritocratic partnership model, SPX Capital seeks to attract and retain highly skilled professionals. The firm’s culture encourages teamwork and rewards those who seek excellence in group results.
Consistent returns and capital preservation are central to the SPX Capital’s ethos. The firm believes in gradual and sustainable growth, with the objective of building a lasting, resilient organization.

## OUR PRINCIPLES
#### Expertise
A culture that promotes specialization and expertise across every area of the firm.
#### Partnership and Meritocracy
A meritocratic partnership with a collaborative culture, where outstanding professionals will be recognized based on results.
#### Discipline and Resilience
Discipline in the management of investments and resilience in the search for long-term performance.
#### Client focus
We manage client capital with the same care and diligence as we do our own.
#### Alignment of Interests
The partners have a large amount of their wealth in the firm’s funds and are required to reinvest a majority of the distributed profits.
#### Ethical behavior
We believe that a strong ethical framework is essential for building a lasting business.

### Our Team
## PARTNERSHIP
## Board of Directors
```
                    Array
(
    [4] => Array
        (
            [213] => Array
                (
                    [nome] => Albano Franco
                    [ID] => 213
                    [slug] => albano-franco-2
                    [setor] => 4
                    [cargo] => Director and Head of EM Credit
                    [descricao] => Joined SPX in 2019. Began his career at Banco Pactual where he stayed for 15 years, becoming partner in 2012.                     [descricao] => Marcelo Castro joined SPX in January 2020 as partner and portfolio manager. His focus is global macro, with emphasis on sovereign credit, currencies, interest rates of emerging market economies. Prior to SPX, he was a partner and portfolio manager at Pharo Management from September 2005 to July 2016, where he helped develop a framework of risk taking heavily reliant on quantitative economic research and portfolio optimization tools. He has also worked at BNP Paribas from 1998 to 2004, Bankers Trust (1993-1997) and Banco Icatu (1989-1993). His focus at these institutions was Latin American fixed income and currency instruments trading, with a research-based, bottom-up approach.

Mr. Castro received his B.S Economics from PUC-Rio in 1990 and a one-year specialization degree in pure mathematics at USP-IME in 2005.  In July 2019 he graduated from LSE with a MSc in Economics.  Additionally, he taught the fundamentals of finance at Ibmec College, São Paulo (2002-2004) and published articles in the _Handbook of Emerging Fixed Income and Currency Markets,_ edited by Fabozzi & Franco in 1998, _Investing in Emerging Fixed Income Markets_, edited by Fabozzi and Pilarinu (2002) and _Risco e Regulacao_ edited by Giambiagi and Garcia (2010).
```

#### Rogério Xavier 
Board of Directors Chairman  
Head of Rates
Founded SPX in 2010 after working for Banco de Investimentos Garantia (1985-88) and Banco BBM (1989-2010), where he was Head of the proprietary trading desk (1997-2007) and Executive Director of the Asset Management (2008-10). Graduated in business administration from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ), he is a board member of the Pontifical Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro Endowment (PUC-RJ) and the Mobility and Social Development Institute (IMDS). 
#### Bruno Marangoni 
Board of Directors  
CEO
Joined SPX as a partner in 2014. Began his career in 2004 as a trainee at Banco Pactual and in 2007 joined the Currencies Desk. Later became portfolio manager for the Currencies and Fixed Income Desk at JGP Gestão de Recursos. Left JGP in 2014. Graduated in production engineering from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). 
#### Bruno Pandolfi 
Board of Directors  
Head of FX
Founded SPX in 2010. Joined Banco BBM in 1996, becoming a partner in 2003. Appointed Chief Financial Officer in 2009. Left Banco BBM in 2010. Earned an MBA with emphasis in finance from Instituto Brasileiro de Mercado de Capitais (IBMEC-RJ). Graduated in electronic engineering from the Federal University of Rio de Janeiro (UFRJ). 
#### Daniel Schneider 
Board of Directors  
Head of Investor Relations
Founded SPX in 2010. Began his career in 1994 in Alcan Brazil’s Financial Department. Joined Banco BBM in 1996 and became a partner in 2003. Appointed Director, Fixed Income Funds, Asset Management, in 2009. Left Banco BBM in 2010. Graduated in business management from Fundação Getúlio Vargas in São Paulo (FGV-SP). 
#### Leonardo Linhares 
Board of Directors  
Head of Equities
Joined SPX as a partner in 2012. Began his career in 1994 at Banco BBM, where he became a partner in 2003. Appointed Director, Equity Funds, Asset Management, in 2009. Left Banco BBM in 2012. Graduated in economics from the Federal University of Rio de Janeiro (UFRJ). 
#### Marcelo Castro 
Board of Directors  
Head of Multi-Asset
Marcelo Castro joined SPX in January 2020 as partner and portfolio manager. His focus is global macro, with emphasis on sovereign credit, currencies, interest rates of emerging market economies. Prior to SPX, he was a partner and portfolio manager at Pharo Management from September 2005 to July 2016, where he helped develop a framework of risk taking heavily reliant on quantitative economic research and portfolio optimization tools. He has also worked at BNP Paribas from 1998 to 2004, Bankers Trust (1993-1997) and Banco Icatu (1989-1993). His focus at these institutions was Latin American fixed income and currency instruments trading, with a research-based, bottom-up approach. Mr. Castro received his B.S Economics from PUC-Rio in 1990 and a one-year specialization degree in pure mathematics at USP-IME in 2005. In July 2019 he graduated from LSE with a MSc in Economics. Additionally, he taught the fundamentals of finance at Ibmec College, São Paulo (2002-2004) and published articles in the  _Handbook of Emerging Fixed Income and Currency Markets,_ edited by Fabozzi & Franco in 1998,  _Investing in Emerging Fixed Income Markets_ , edited by Fabozzi and Pilarinu (2002) and  _Risco e Regulacao_ edited by Giambiagi and Garcia (2010). 
* * *
## Partners
#### Albano Franco 
Director and Head of EM Credit
Joined SPX in 2019. Began his career at Banco Pactual where he stayed for 15 years, becoming partner in 2012. Worked in the equity research team covering retail and food sectors. Joined UBS Pactual’s proprietary credit desk before assuming in 2008 as head of BTG Pactual Asset Management’s credit area, being responsible for all credit strategies and its dedicated funds. Worked at American Express Financial Advisors in Atlanta, USA. Franco holds a degree in finance from Georgia State University. 
#### Alexandre Rodrigues 
Multi-Strategy PM
Joined SPX in 2024, in the São Paulo’s office as a Partner at Multi-Strategy area. Alexandre has previous experience at Itaú, Canvas Capital, Banco Pan, BTG Pactual and Banco Brascan. He holds a degree in Electronic Engineering at Universidade Federal do Rio de Janeiro (UFRJ) and earned a master's degree in Economics at Instituto de Ensino e Pesquisa (INSPER). 
#### Beny Parnes 
Chief Economist North American & Asia
Joined SPX as a partner in 2013. Began his career at Banco BBM in 1991. Board member Head of the Central Bank of Brazil’s International Affairs Department between 2002 and 2003. Returned to Banco BBM in 2004 as an executive director and left again in 2013. Completed the credits for the doctoral program at the University of Pennsylvania (without concluding his thesis). Graduated in economics from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). Senior lecturer at this university’s Department of Economics. 
#### Bernardo Queiroz 
Director of Operations and Products, COO
Joined SPX as a partner in 2010. Began his career at Banco BBM’s back office in 2003. Left Banco BBM in 2010. Earned an MBA with emphasis in finance and capital markets from Fundação Getúlio Vargas (FGV-RJ). Graduated in business administration from Instituto Brasileiro de Mercado de Capitais (IBMEC-RJ). 
#### Bernardo Remy 
Investor Relations
Joined SPX as a partner in 2021. Before SPX, he worked at Pátria Investimentos, Bratus Capital, Partners Group and Aracruz Celulose. Remy earned an MBA from London Business School and a Bachelor’s Degree in Business Administration from Ibmec – RJ. 
#### Bruna Silveira 
Head of Equities Research
Joined SPX in 2012, becoming a partner in 2014. Began her career at Banco BBM in 2010, working in the Equities sector. In 2011, worked as Market Analyst. Graduated in Economics from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). 
#### Bruno Mafra 
Head of Quant
Joined SPX as a partner in 2010. Began his career at Banco BBM in 2004. Appointed portfolio manager of commodities desk in 2009. Left Banco BBM in 2010. Earned a master’s in finance from Instituto Nacional de Matemática Pura e Aplicada (IMPA). Graduated in electrical engineering from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ) and École Centrale de Paris. 
#### Diego Andrés 
Head of Quant Research
Joined SPX in 2019 as a quantitative analyst. He was a co-founder of Trapezus Asset Management in 2010 and partner at Bozano Investimentos / Crescera Investimentos. Diego holds a degree in Electronic Engineering from Instituto Militar de Engenharia (IME). He has a master degree in Mathematical Methods Applied to Finance at Instituto de Matemática Pura e Aplicada (IMPA). 
#### Edson Peli 
Director of Private Equity
Joined SPX in 2021 as a partner in Private Equity. Edson was a Managing Director at The Carlyle Group focused on private equity investments in South America, primarily in Brazil, for over 13 years. Since 2008 at Carlyle, he has directly participated in more than R$ 5 billion in equity investments from Carlyle’s funds in the healthcare, education and consumer & retail sectors. Prior to Carlyle, Edson worked in investment banking at Credit Suisse in Brazil from 2004 to 2008, where he participated in several M&A and IPO transactions across various sectors. Prior to that, Edson worked in credit risk analysis at Citi from 2002 to 2004. Edson graduated in Business Administration at Fundação Getúlio Vargas (FGV) and holds a Certificate of Specialization in Corporate Finance & Capital Markets at The University of Texas at Austin.
#### Eduardo Zilberman 
Senior Economist LatAm and Asia
Joined SPX in 2024 in the Rio de Janeiro’s office as a Partner and Latam Senior Economist at Macro area. Eduardo has previous experience at Gávea Investimentos, PUC and Central Bank of Chile. He holds a degree and a master’s in Economics from Pontifícia Universidade Católica (PUC) and a doctorate in Economics from New York University (NYU). 
#### Federico Favero 
Head of IT and Technology
Joined SPX in 2019 an analyst at Credit Risk Area. He has previous experience at Brain Brane (Italy), Snell Habitat SPA (Italy), Evolutiq GMBH (Swiss), Banco BBM (Brazil). Federico graduated in Pure and Applied Mathematics at Universitá Degli Studi di Padova (Italy), he is also post-graduated in Advanced Risk and Portfolio Management (ARPM Bootcamp) from NY University (USA), and holds a Master’s Advanced Finance from IE Business School (Spain). 
#### Fernando Borges 
Director and Head of Private Equity
Joined SPX in 2021 as partner and head of Private Equity. Fernando was Head of Carlyle South America Buyout. He has 25 years of private equity experience in Brazil, having participated in over 20 transactions and served on many of the boards of Carlyle’s local portfolio companies. He is also a former Chairman of ABVCAP, the Brazilian Private Equity & Venture Capital Association. Prior to joining Carlyle, Fernando was Managing Director of AIG Capital Partners and CEO of AIG Capital Investments do Brasil, responsible for managing AIG’s private equity assets in Brazil. From 1994 to 1999, he was a Principal of Bozano, Simonsen’s private equity division. Fernando graduated in International Relations at Universidade de Brasília (UnB). 
#### Gabriel Hartung 
Head of Rates Brazil
Joined SPX as a partner in 2013. Began his career at Instituto Brasileiro de Economia (IBRE) in 2006. Joined Banco BBM’s Macroeconomic Research team in 2008, leaving in 2013. Earned a PhD and master’s from Fundação Getúlio Vargas (EPGE/FGV). Graduated in economics from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). 
#### Guilherme Mazie 
CFO
Joined SPX in 2012, becoming a partner in 2013. Began his career at Banco BBM in 2009, researching quantitative models. Appointed equities fund portfolio manager in 2011. Left Banco BBM in 2012. Graduated in production engineering from the Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). 
#### Gustavo Rabello 
FX Senior PM
Joined SPX in 2015 on the Macroeconomic Research Team and later became a currency analyst. In 2017 became a Currency Trader. Rabello holds a master’s degree in Economics from Getúlio Vargas Foundation (FGV) and graduated in Economics from the Federal University of Rio de Janeiro (UFRJ). 
#### James Brilliant 
Legal & Compliance Senior Manager
Joined SPX in 2017. From 2012 to 2017, he held senior compliance positions at Nomura International, Capula Investment Management and Winton Capital, and from 2004 to 2012 he practised as a regulatory lawyer, first at the English Bar and then with law firms Shearman & Sterling and Kirkland & Ellis. Graduated from Oxford University with a degree in Classics. 
#### James Eckrich 
Investor Relations
Joined SPX in 2017 and became a partner in 2022. Began his career at Morgan Stanley in NY and in 2009 was transferred to London. In 2012 he joined the investor relations team at JGP Global, working out of their headquarters in Rio de Janeiro. Mr. Eckrich graduated with a degree in Business Administration and Finance from University of Richmond, USA. 
#### João Faria 
Senior Economist Europe
Joined SPX in 2015. Started his career as Projectl Manager at the Ministry of Development, Industry and Foreign Trade. He holds a degree in International Relations from UnB and a Masters in Economics from EPGE / FGV. 
#### João Victor Torres 
Equities Longs Senior PM
Joined SPX in 2016. He started his career with an internship in the stock exchange area. João holds a degree in Economics from PUC Rio. 
#### Katherine Albuquerque 
Director of Legal and Compliance, GC & CCO
Joined SPX as a partner in 2014. Began her career at Banco BBM in 1997, working in Corporate / Fiscal areas. In 2009 joined EBX working initially the Legal Department, as well as in the banking, corporate and tax areas. Earned an MBA with emphasis in finance and specialization in tax law from Getúlio Vargas Foundation (FGV-RJ). Graduated in law school from Catholic University of Rio de Janeiro (PUC-RJ). 
#### Kym Ardison 
Currency Senior PM
Joined SPX in 2017. Began her career as an intern at Ativa Corretora. Worked at Dimensional Fund Advisors (Texas) in the summer internship program for PhDs. Ardison has a degree in Economics from FUCAPE Business School, a master’s and a PhD in Economics from Brazilian School of Economics and Finance (EPGE – FGV). 
#### Leonardo Cabral 
Director of Risk and Pricing, CRO

Worked in London at Deutsche Bank (2004-2009) in the FX derivatives trading desk and at Barclays as director of the FX Correlation trading desk. In 2011, returned to Brazil as a partner at JGP Gestão de Recursos, working as Senior Curriencies Portfolio Manager. Earned an MBA from Wharton – University of Pennsylvania – with emphasis in finance and accounting in 2005. Graduated in Mechanical Engeneering from the Federal University of Rio de Janeiro (UFRJ).

## Termos e Condições do Website
Abaixo seguem algumas informações importantes sobre o material contido no website:  
  
As informações contidas neste website são de caráter meramente informativo e não constituem qualquer tipo de aconselhamento de investimentos, não devendo ser utilizadas para esta finalidade. Seu único propósito é dar transparência à gestão executada pela SPX Gestão de Recursos Ltda. (“SPX Capital”), SPX Private Equity Gestão de Recursos Ltda. (“SPX Private Equity”), SPX SYN Gestão de Recursos Ltda. (“SPX SYN”), SPX Soluções de Investimentos Ltda. ("SPX Soluções de Investimentos") e empresas do grupo SPX (“Grupo SPX”).  
  
Nenhuma informação contida neste website constitui uma solicitação, oferta ou recomendação para compra ou venda de quotas de fundos de investimento, ou de quaisquer outros valores mobiliários. O Grupo SPX não comercializa nem distribui quotas de fundos de investimento ou qualquer outro ativo financeiro. Recomendamos uma consulta a assessores de investimento e profissionais especializados para uma análise específica, personalizada antes de sua decisão sobre investimentos.  
  
Aos investidores, é recomendada a leitura cuidadosa de prospectos e regulamentos ao aplicar seus recursos.  
  
Este website não é direcionado para quem se encontrar proibido por lei a acessar as informações nele contidas, as quais não devem ser usadas de qualquer forma contrária a qualquer lei de qualquer jurisdição.  
  
Fundos de Investimento não contam com a garantia do administrador do fundo, do gestor da carteira, de qualquer mecanismo de seguro ou, ainda, do Fundo Garantidor de Créditos – FGC.  
  
Nos fundos geridos pelo Grupo SPX, a data de conversão de cotas pode ser diversa da data de aplicação e de resgate, e a data de pagamento do resgate pode ser diversa da data do pedido de resgate.  
  
A rentabilidade divulgada em determinados trechos do website já é líquida das taxas de administração, de performance e dos outros custos pertinentes ao fundo, mas não é líquida de impostos. Para avaliação da performance do fundo de investimento, é recomendável uma análise de, no mínimo, 12 (doze) meses. A rentabilidade obtida no passado não representa garantia de rentabilidade futura.  
  
Os fundos geridos pelo Grupo SPX podem utilizar estratégias com derivativos como parte integrante de sua política de investimento. Tais estratégias, da forma como são adotadas, podem resultar em significativas perdas patrimoniais para seus cotistas, podendo, inclusive, acarretar tanto perdas superiores ao capital aplicado, quanto uma consequente obrigação do cotista de aportar recursos adicionais para cobrir o prejuízo do fundo.  
  
Eventuais fundos geridos pelo Grupo SPX estão autorizados a realizar aplicações em ativos financeiros no exterior. Os fundos podem ainda estar expostos a uma significativa concentração em ativos de poucos emissores, com riscos daí decorrentes. Não há garantia de que os fundos multimercados terão o tratamento tributário para fundos de longo prazo.  
  
O Grupo SPX, seus administradores, sócios e funcionários não se responsabilizam pela publicação acidental de informações incorretas, e isentam-se de responsabilidade sobre quaisquer danos resultantes direta ou indiretamente da utilização das informações contidas neste website.  
  
O conteúdo deste website não pode ser copiado, reproduzido, publicado, retransmitido ou distribuído, no todo ou em parte, por qualquer meio e modo, sem a prévia e expressa autorização, por escrito, do Grupo SPX. 
concordo  não concordo

### fundos / ações
# Falcon 2
Descrição e características Dados estatísticos Performance Arquivos
## Descrição e características
#### Objetivo
Fundo de ações com objetivo de proporcionar aos seus cotistas ganhos de capital no longo prazo.
#### Política de Investimento
Fundo de ações _long bias_ com mandato flexível em sua exposição ao mercado de ações. Estratégia focada em valor e ciclos econômicos, combinando _stock-picking_ e _market timing_. O risco predominante do fundo vem da carteira comprada em ações brasileiras, sendo complementado através de uma carteira vendida, _long and shorts_ específicos, posições em bolsas internacionais e em outros mercados macro, com objetivo também de proteção, atenuando a volatilidade do fundo ao longo dos ciclos e buscando um melhor retorno ajustado ao risco.
O Fundo pode manter até 40% dos seus recursos no exterior.
#### Público Alvo
Investidores qualificados que busquem performance diferenciada e entendam a natureza e a extensão dos riscos envolvidos.
#### Informações Gerais
Data de Início 12/09/2022*  
Classificação Anbima Ações Livre  
Aplicação Inicial Mínima R$ 5.000,00  
Movimentação mínima R$ 5.000,00  
Saldo Mínimo R$ 5.000,00  
Horário Mínimo 15:30  
Cota de Aplicação Cota do dia útil subsequente à disponibilidade dos recursos (D+1)  
Cota de Resgate Cota de D+30 dias corridos após a solicitação do resgate  
Pagamento do Resgate 2º dia útil subsequente à conversão de cotas  
Taxa de Administração 2.0% a.a.¹  
Taxa de Performance 20% do que exceder IPCA + Yield IMA-B  
Gestores SPX Gestão de Recursos Ltda.  
Administrador Intrag Distribuidora de Títulos e Valores Mobiliários Ltda  
Tributação  15% na fonte sobre o ganho nominal  
1 Taxa de administração total de 2,00% a.a., sendo 0,70% a.a. incidente sobre os investimentos no SPX Falcon 2 FIC FIA, acrescido de 1,30% a.a. incidente sobre os investimentos do SPX Falcon 2 FIC FIA no SPX Falcon Master FIA.
*Início da estratégia em 14/09/2012

## Termos e Condições do Website
Abaixo seguem algumas informações importantes sobre o material contido no website:  
  
As informações contidas neste website são de caráter meramente informativo e não constituem qualquer tipo de aconselhamento de investimentos, não devendo ser utilizadas para esta finalidade. Seu único propósito é dar transparência à gestão executada pela SPX Gestão de Recursos Ltda. (“SPX Capital”), SPX Private Equity Gestão de Recursos Ltda. (“SPX Private Equity”), SPX SYN Gestão de Recursos Ltda. (“SPX SYN”), SPX Soluções de Investimentos Ltda. ("SPX Soluções de Investimentos") e empresas do grupo SPX (“Grupo SPX”).  
  
Nenhuma informação contida neste website constitui uma solicitação, oferta ou recomendação para compra ou venda de quotas de fundos de investimento, ou de quaisquer outros valores mobiliários. O Grupo SPX não comercializa nem distribui quotas de fundos de investimento ou qualquer outro ativo financeiro. Recomendamos uma consulta a assessores de investimento e profissionais especializados para uma análise específica, personalizada antes de sua decisão sobre investimentos.  
  
Aos investidores, é recomendada a leitura cuidadosa de prospectos e regulamentos ao aplicar seus recursos.  
  
Este website não é direcionado para quem se encontrar proibido por lei a acessar as informações nele contidas, as quais não devem ser usadas de qualquer forma contrária a qualquer lei de qualquer jurisdição.  
  
Fundos de Investimento não contam com a garantia do administrador do fundo, do gestor da carteira, de qualquer mecanismo de seguro ou, ainda, do Fundo Garantidor de Créditos – FGC.  
  
Nos fundos geridos pelo Grupo SPX, a data de conversão de cotas pode ser diversa da data de aplicação e de resgate, e a data de pagamento do resgate pode ser diversa da data do pedido de resgate.  
  
A rentabilidade divulgada em determinados trechos do website já é líquida das taxas de administração, de performance e dos outros custos pertinentes ao fundo, mas não é líquida de impostos. Para avaliação da performance do fundo de investimento, é recomendável uma análise de, no mínimo, 12 (doze) meses. A rentabilidade obtida no passado não representa garantia de rentabilidade futura.  
  
Os fundos geridos pelo Grupo SPX podem utilizar estratégias com derivativos como parte integrante de sua política de investimento. Tais estratégias, da forma como são adotadas, podem resultar em significativas perdas patrimoniais para seus cotistas, podendo, inclusive, acarretar tanto perdas superiores ao capital aplicado, quanto uma consequente obrigação do cotista de aportar recursos adicionais para cobrir o prejuízo do fundo.  
  
Eventuais fundos geridos pelo Grupo SPX estão autorizados a realizar aplicações em ativos financeiros no exterior. Os fundos podem ainda estar expostos a uma significativa concentração em ativos de poucos emissores, com riscos daí decorrentes. Não há garantia de que os fundos multimercados terão o tratamento tributário para fundos de longo prazo.  
  
O Grupo SPX, seus administradores, sócios e funcionários não se responsabilizam pela publicação acidental de informações incorretas, e isentam-se de responsabilidade sobre quaisquer danos resultantes direta ou indiretamente da utilização das informações contidas neste website.  
  
O conteúdo deste website não pode ser copiado, reproduzido, publicado, retransmitido ou distribuído, no todo ou em parte, por qualquer meio e modo, sem a prévia e expressa autorização, por escrito, do Grupo SPX.

### fundos / ações
# Apache
Descrição e características Dados estatísticos Performance Arquivos
## Descrição e características
#### Objetivo
Fundo de ações com objetivo de proporcionar aos seus cotistas ganhos de capital no longo prazo.
#### Política de Investimento
Fundo segue a mesma estratégia do SPX Patriot, respeitando a regulamentação das EFPCs (Entidades Fechadas de Previdência Complementar).
Fundo de ações _long only_ com estratégia focada em valor e ciclos econômicos, combinando _stock-picking_ e _market timing_ na escolha de ações, a partir de análise fundamentalista profunda.
Os investimentos são realizados a partir de uma sólida abordagem micro e macroeconômica e de uma rigorosa avaliação dos riscos envolvidos.
#### Público Alvo
Investidores institucionais que busquem performance diferenciada e entendam a natureza e a extensão dos riscos envolvidos.
#### Informações Gerais
Data de Início 18/10/2012  
Classificação Anbima Ações Livre  
Aplicação Inicial Mínima  R$ 5.000,00   
Movimentação mínima  R$ 5.000,00   
Saldo Mínimo  R$ 5.000,00   
Horário Mínimo  15:30   
Cota de Aplicação  Cota do dia útil subsequente à disponibilidade dos recursos (D+1)   
Cota de Resgate  Cota de D+30 dias corridos após a solicitação do resgate   
Pagamento do Resgate  2º dia útil subsequente à conversão de cotas   
Taxa de Antecipação de Resgate  5%¹  
Taxa de Administração  2.0% a.a.²  
Taxa de Performance  20% do que exceder o diferencial do IBX   
Gestores  SPX Gestão de Recursos Ltda.   
Administrador  Intrag Distribuidora de Títulos e Valores Mobiliários Ltda   
Tributação  15% na fonte sobre o ganho nominal   
¹Incidente sobre os valores resgatados. Nessas condições a quotização será no dia do recebimento do pedido com pagamento no dia útil subsequente.
²Taxa de administração total de 2,00% a.a., sendo 1,90% a.a. incidente sobre os investimentos no SPX Apache FIC FIA, acrescido de 0,10% a.a. investimentos do SPX Apache Master FIA.

## Termos e Condições do Website
Abaixo seguem algumas informações importantes sobre o material contido no website:  
  
As informações contidas neste website são de caráter meramente informativo e não constituem qualquer tipo de aconselhamento de investimentos, não devendo ser utilizadas para esta finalidade. Seu único propósito é dar transparência à gestão executada pela SPX Gestão de Recursos Ltda. (“SPX Capital”), SPX Private Equity Gestão de Recursos Ltda. (“SPX Private Equity”), SPX SYN Gestão de Recursos Ltda. (“SPX SYN”), SPX Soluções de Investimentos Ltda. ("SPX Soluções de Investimentos") e empresas do grupo SPX (“Grupo SPX”).  
  
Nenhuma informação contida neste website constitui uma solicitação, oferta ou recomendação para compra ou venda de quotas de fundos de investimento, ou de quaisquer outros valores mobiliários. O Grupo SPX não comercializa nem distribui quotas de fundos de investimento ou qualquer outro ativo financeiro. Recomendamos uma consulta a assessores de investimento e profissionais especializados para uma análise específica, personalizada antes de sua decisão sobre investimentos.  
  
Aos investidores, é recomendada a leitura cuidadosa de prospectos e regulamentos ao aplicar seus recursos.  
  
Este website não é direcionado para quem se encontrar proibido por lei a acessar as informações nele contidas, as quais não devem ser usadas de qualquer forma contrária a qualquer lei de qualquer jurisdição.  
  
Fundos de Investimento não contam com a garantia do administrador do fundo, do gestor da carteira, de qualquer mecanismo de seguro ou, ainda, do Fundo Garantidor de Créditos – FGC.  
  
Nos fundos geridos pelo Grupo SPX, a data de conversão de cotas pode ser diversa da data de aplicação e de resgate, e a data de pagamento do resgate pode ser diversa da data do pedido de resgate.  
  
A rentabilidade divulgada em determinados trechos do website já é líquida das taxas de administração, de performance e dos outros custos pertinentes ao fundo, mas não é líquida de impostos. Para avaliação da performance do fundo de investimento, é recomendável uma análise de, no mínimo, 12 (doze) meses. A rentabilidade obtida no passado não representa garantia de rentabilidade futura.  
  
Os fundos geridos pelo Grupo SPX podem utilizar estratégias com derivativos como parte integrante de sua política de investimento. Tais estratégias, da forma como são adotadas, podem resultar em significativas perdas patrimoniais para seus cotistas, podendo, inclusive, acarretar tanto perdas superiores ao capital aplicado, quanto uma consequente obrigação do cotista de aportar recursos adicionais para cobrir o prejuízo do fundo.  
  
Eventuais fundos geridos pelo Grupo SPX estão autorizados a realizar aplicações em ativos financeiros no exterior. Os fundos podem ainda estar expostos a uma significativa concentração em ativos de poucos emissores, com riscos daí decorrentes. Não há garantia de que os fundos multimercados terão o tratamento tributário para fundos de longo prazo.  
  
O Grupo SPX, seus administradores, sócios e funcionários não se responsabilizam pela publicação acidental de informações incorretas, e isentam-se de responsabilidade sobre quaisquer danos resultantes direta ou indiretamente da utilização das informações contidas neste website.  
  
O conteúdo deste website não pode ser copiado, reproduzido, publicado, retransmitido ou distribuído, no todo ou em parte, por qualquer meio e modo, sem a prévia e expressa autorização, por escrito, do Grupo SPX.

### fundos / ações
# Falcon
Descrição e características Dados estatísticos Performance Arquivos
## Descrição e características
#### Objetivo
Fundo de ações com objetivo de proporcionar aos seus cotistas ganhos de capital no longo prazo.
#### Política de Investimento
Fundo de ações _long bias_ com mandato flexível em sua exposição ao mercado de ações. Estratégia focada em valor e ciclos econômicos, combinando _stock-picking_ e _market timing_. O risco predominante do fundo vem da carteira comprada em ações brasileiras, sendo complementado através de uma carteira vendida, _long and shorts_ específicos, posições em bolsas internacionais e em outros mercados macro, com objetivo também de proteção, atenuando a volatilidade do fundo ao longo dos ciclos e buscando um melhor retorno ajustado ao risco.
O Fundo pode manter até 40% dos seus recursos no exterior.
#### Público Alvo
Investidores qualificados que busquem performance diferenciada e entendam a natureza e a extensão dos riscos envolvidos.
#### Informações Gerais
Data de Início* 14/09/2012  
Classificação Anbima Ações Livre  
Aplicação Inicial Mínima R$ 5.000,00  
Movimentação mínima R$ 5.000,00  
Saldo Mínimo R$ 5.000,00  
Horário Mínimo 15:30  
Cota de Aplicação Cota do dia útil subsequente à disponibilidade dos recursos (D+1)  
Cota de Resgate Cota de D+30 dias corridos após a solicitação do resgate  
Pagamento do Resgate 2º dia útil subsequente à conversão de cotas  
Taxa de Antecipação de Resgate 10%¹  
Taxa de Administração 2.0% a.a.²  
Taxa de Performance 20% do que exceder IPCA + 6%  
Gestores SPX Gestão de Recursos Ltda.  
Administrador Intrag Distribuidora de Títulos e Valores Mobiliários Ltda  
Tributação  15% na fonte sobre o ganho nominal  
1 Incidente sobre os valores resgatados. Nessas condições a quotização será no dia do recebimento do pedido com pagamento no dia útil subsequente.  
2 Taxa de administração total de 2,00% a.a., sendo 0,70% a.a. incidente sobre os investimentos no SPX Falcon FIC FIA, acrescidode 1,30% a.a. incidente sobre os investimentos do SPX Falcon FIC FIA no SPX Falcon Master FIA.
